class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;No&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back7f721940-8d21-11e6-b79f-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#7f721940-8d21-11e6-b79f-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#c28ea390-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#7f721940-8d21-11e6-b79f-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;c2961da0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;HP-UX&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;The first step is to identify the admin console process ID. You can run the below command to find the admin console PID:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;&lt;em&gt;ps -fe | grep &amp;lt;username&amp;gt; | grep _AdminConsole&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Contrary to the popular belief Admin console process CAN run on a non-mastergateway node as well (it however CANNOT run on a worker node), so if the domain had multiple gateway nodes, please check for the admin console process on all the gateway nodes if we are unable to find it on the master gateway.&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Next step is to find the PID of the node java process of the master gateway node(If the admin console is running on a non-masterGateway node also get the Process ID of the node process of that node. This would be the parent process of the admin console process). Refer to the KB &lt;a title=&quot;147825 find node java PID&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/147825.aspx?myk=147825&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;147825&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;to get the PID of the node java process of the master gateway node&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Once you have the PIDs, run the following diagnostics:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -p &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at an interval of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmap &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; pmap_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span&gt;jstack &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; jstack_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;gencore &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file generated in the above step. Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;http://psv28cmsmas1:7000/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more information.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pfiles &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; pfiles_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span&gt;tusc -f -r all -w all -o tusc_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;.out -p &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Let this run for around two minutes and then exit.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Collect the following(these do not require a process ID)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;netstat &amp;gt; netstat_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt; Taken at least three times&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;vmstat 5 5 &amp;gt; vmstat_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;iostat 5 5 &amp;gt; iostat_otput&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;top&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;&amp;ndash;d 5 &amp;ndash;n 5 &amp;gt; top_out&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;sar -A &amp;gt; sar_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;/&lt;span&gt;var/adm/syslog/syslog.log&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Collect the following logs:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>infa9Logs on all the nodes of the domain. click &lt;a title=&quot;infa9Logs&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/147882.aspx?myk=147882&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for details on the utility.  </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;gcore, pmap, pfiles, tusc, netstat, vmstat, top, sar, are all HP-UX system utilities. In case of any issues, contact your system admins.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;pmstack is available under $INFA_HOME/tools/debugtools/pmstack directory in Informatica installations version 9.5.x and above. For other versions it could be downloaded from &lt;a title=&quot;pmstack&quot; href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/docs/DOC-7327&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here.&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;jstack is present in&lt;em&gt; $JAVA_HOME/bin/ &lt;/em&gt;directory&lt;/span&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Did you face any issues while collecting the above?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#c294be10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c2961da0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backc294be10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#c2961da0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Yes&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#c294e520-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c2961da0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backc294e520-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#c2961da0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;No&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backc2961da0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c2961da0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#c28ea390-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c2961da0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;47302920-8d1f-11e6-b79f-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;HP-UX&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;The first step is to get the Process ID(PID) of the Integration service(or the PIDs if the Integration service runs on a GRID).&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If there is just one integration service running on the server you can easily get the PID by logging into the machine and checking for the running processes. The integration service runs as a &quot;pmserver&quot; process. If there are multiple integration service processes you can get the Process ID from the admin console's &quot;Logs&quot; tab. Just filter the logs for the integration service in question here and then add the &quot;Node&quot; and &quot;Process&quot; columns to the already available columns in the log window(you can do that by doing a Right click on any of the columns viz. Service Type, Service Name etc and then clicking on Columns). This would give you the node on which the process is running as well as the Process ID with which the service is running. Please refer to KB &lt;a title=&quot;KB151366_Find_PID&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/151366.aspx?myk=151366&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;151366&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for other options. If the Integration service runs on a GRID, please get the pmserver process for all the nodes of the Grid using the admin console.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Next, we need to get the PID of the associated repository service. The Repository service the IS is associated to can be found from the admin console. Click on the IS in the domain navigator and then click on the &quot;Associated Repository&quot; tab.&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;If there is just one repository service running on the server you can easily get the PID by logging into the machine and checking for the running processes. The repository service runs as a &quot;pmrepagent&quot; process. If there are multiple Repository service processes you can get the Process ID from the admin console's &quot;Logs&quot; tab. Just filter the logs for the repository service in question here and then add the &quot;Node&quot; and &quot;Process&quot; columns to the already available columns in the log window(you can do that by doing a Right click on any of the columns viz. Service Type, Service Name etc and then clicking on Columns). This would give you the node on which the process is running as well as the Process ID with which the service is running. Please refer to KB &lt;/span&gt;&lt;a title=&quot;KB151366_Find_PID&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/151366.aspx?myk=151366&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;151366&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;for other options.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;We also need to get the Process ID of the node java process. You can login to the node running the master gateway process and get the PID of a java process which is the Parent of the integration service process that we just found and that would be the PID of the node java. If you have a multinode setup and the integration service is running on a node other than the master gateway, you would require multiple Process IDs, for the parent of the pmserver(s) and pmrepagent we just found and for the node java process of the master gateway node. For more details on how to get the PID, please refer to KB &lt;a title=&quot;147825 find node java PID&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/147825.aspx?myk=147825&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;147825&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Once you have the PID of the pmrepagent process, pmserver process(es) and the &lt;strong&gt;node java process, following should be run:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Execute the following on the PID of the pmrepagent process, pmserver process(es) and the node java process(es).&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -p -d dbx &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at an interval of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmap &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; pmap_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jstack &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; jstack_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt; (ONLY ON THE NODE JAVA AND NOT THE REPOSITORY OR INTEGRATION SERVICE)&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;gencore &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file generated in the above step. Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;http://psv28cmsmas1:7000/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more information.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pfiles &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; pfiles_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;t&lt;span&gt;usc -f -r all -w all -o tusc_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;.out -p &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Let this run for around two minutes and then exit.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Collect the following(these do not require a process ID)&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;netstat &amp;gt; netstat_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt; Taken at least three times&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;vmstat 5 5 &amp;gt; vmstat_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;iostat 5 5 &amp;gt; iostat_otput&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;top&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;&amp;ndash;d 5 &amp;ndash;n 5 &amp;gt; top_out&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;sar -A &amp;gt; sar_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;/&lt;span&gt;var/adm/syslog/syslog.log&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Collect the following logs:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Integration service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;gcore, pmap, pfiles, tusc, netstat, vmstat, top, sar, are all HP-UX system utilities. In case of any issues, contact your system admins.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;pmstack is available under $INFA_HOME/tools/debugtools/pmstack directory in Informatica installations version 9.5.x and above. For other versions it could be downloaded from &lt;a title=&quot;pmstack&quot; href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/docs/DOC-7327&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here.&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;jstack is present in $JAVA_HOME/bin/ directory.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Did you face any issues while collecting the above?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#c294be10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#47302920-8d1f-11e6-b79f-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backc294be10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#47302920-8d1f-11e6-b79f-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;c2909f60-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;No&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backc2909f60-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c2909f60-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#c28ea390-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c2909f60-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;c2972f10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Windows&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;The first step is to get the Process ID(PID) of the repository service. If there is just one repository service running on the server you can easily get the PID by logging into the machine and checking for the running processes. The repository service runs as a &quot;pmrepagent&quot; process. If there are multiple Repository service processes you can get the Process ID from the admin console's &quot;Logs&quot; tab. Just filter the logs for the repository service in question here and then add the &quot;Node&quot; and &quot;Process&quot; columns to the already available columns in the log window(you can do that by doing a Right click on any of the columns viz. Service Type, Service Name etc and then clicking on Columns). This would give you the node on which the process is running as well as the Process ID with which the service is running. Please refer to KB &lt;a title=&quot;KB151366_Find_PID&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/151366.aspx?myk=151366&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;151366&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for other options.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;We also need to get the Process ID of the node java process. You can login to the node running the master gateway process and get the PID of a java process which is the Parent of the repository service process that we just found and that would be the PID of the node java. If you have a multinode setup and the repository service is running on a node other than the master gateway, you would require two Process IDs, one for the parent of the pmrepagent we just found and the other for the node java process of the master gateway node. For more details on how to get the PID, please refer to KB &lt;a title=&quot;147825 find node java PID&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/147825.aspx?myk=147825&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;147825.&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Once you have the PID of the pmrepagent process and the &lt;strong&gt;&lt;strong&gt;node java process, following should be run:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Execute the following on the PID of the pmrepagent process and the node java process.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Collect&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;process dumps on the process at least three time at an interval of 2 minutes.&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span&gt;Right&lt;/span&gt;-click on the        Windows Task Bar and select&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Task        Manager...&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;span&gt;from the list.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Right-click on the        process and then click on &quot;Create Dump File&quot;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click &lt;a title=&quot;142454&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/3/Pages/142454.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; to take jstack on the node java process(Not on repository service process)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Collect the following(&lt;span&gt;these do not require a process ID&lt;/span&gt;)    </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Event viewer       logs. Please click &lt;a title=&quot;423971_EventViewer&quot; href=&quot;http://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/18/423971.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span&gt; for guidance.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Resource       utilization report from the machine. You would need to contact to your       System admin for these&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Collect the following logs:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Did you face any issues while collecting the above?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#c294be10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c2972f10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backc294be10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#c2972f10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; If you have a multinode setup and the repository service is running on a node other than the master gateway, you would require two Process IDs, one for the parent of the pmrepagent we just found and the other for the node java process of the master gateway node. For more details on how to get the PID, please refer to KB &lt;a title=&quot;147825 find node java PID&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/147825.aspx?myk=147825&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;147825.&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Once you have the PID of the pmrepagent process and the node java process, following diagnostics should be run:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Execute the following on the PID of the pmrepagent process and the node java process.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -p &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at an interval of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmap &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; pmap_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt; &lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jstack &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; jstack_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt; (ONLY ON THE NODE JAVA AND NOT THE REPOSITORY)&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;gencore &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file generated in the above step. Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;http://psv28cmsmas1:7000/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more information.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pfiles &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; pfiles_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span&gt;tusc -f -r all -w all -o tusc_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;.out -p &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;/span&gt; (ONLY ON THE REPOSITORY AND NOT THE NODE JAVA)&lt;br /&gt;Let this run for around two minutes and then exit.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt; &lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Collect the following(these do not require a process ID)&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;netstat &amp;gt; netstat_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt; Taken at least three times&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;vmstat 5 5 &amp;gt; vmstat_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;iostat 5 5 &amp;gt; iostat_otput&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;t&lt;span&gt;op &amp;ndash;d 5 &amp;ndash;n 5 &amp;gt; top_out&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;sar -A &amp;gt; sar_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;/&lt;span&gt;var/adm/syslog/syslog.log&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Collect the following logs:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;pmap, gcore, pfiles, tusc, netstat, vmstat, top, sar, are all HP-UX system utilities. In case of any issues, contact your system admins.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;pmstack is available under $INFA_HOME/tools/debugtools/pmstack directory in Informatica installations version 9.5.x and above. For other versions it could be downloaded from &lt;a title=&quot;pmstack&quot; href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/docs/DOC-7327&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here.&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;jstack is present in $JAVA_HOME/bin/ directory.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Did you face any issues while collecting the above?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#c294be10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c296e0f0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backc294be10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#c296e0f0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Yes&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#c294e520-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c296e0f0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backc294e520-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#c296e0f0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;No&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backc296e0f0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c296e0f0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#c28ea390-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c296e0f0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;c291b0d0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Solaris/SunOS&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#c297cb50-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c291b0d0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backc297cb50-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#c291b0d0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;The first step is to get the Process ID(PID) of the repository service. If there is just one repository service running on the server you can easily get the PID by logging into the machine and checking for the running processes. The repository service runs as a &quot;pmrepagent&quot; process. If there are multiple Repository service processes you can get the Process ID from the admin console's &quot;Logs&quot; tab. Just filter the logs for the repository service in question here and then add the &quot;Node&quot; and &quot;Process&quot; columns to the already available columns in the log window(you can do that by doing a Right click on any of the columns viz. Service Type, Service Name etc and then clicking on Columns). This would give you the node on which the process is running as well as the Process ID with which the service is running. Please refer to KB &lt;a title=&quot;KB151366_Find_PID&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/151366.aspx?myk=151366&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;151366&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for other options.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;We also need to get the Process ID of the node java process. You can login to the node running the master gateway process and get the PID of a java process which is the Parent of the repository service process that we just found and that would be the PID of the node java. If you have a multinode setup and the repository service is running on a node other than the master gateway, you would require two Process IDs, one for the parent of the pmrepagent we just found and the other for the node java process of the master gateway node. For more details on how to get the PID, please refer to KB &lt;a title=&quot;147825 find node java PID&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/147825.aspx?myk=147825&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;147825.&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Once you have the PID of the pmrepagent process and the node java process, following should be run:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Execute the following on the PID of the pmrepagent process and the node java process:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -p -d dbx &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at an interval of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmap &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; pmap_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jstack &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; jstack_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt; (ONLY ON THE NODE JAVA AND NOT THE REPOSITORY)&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;gcore &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file generated in the above step. Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;http://psv28cmsmas1:7000/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more information. &lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jmap -dump:format=b,file=heapdump.core.&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;lt;EXECUTABLE NAME AND PATH&amp;gt; &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt; (ONLY ON THE NODE JAVA CORE FILE AND NOT THE REPOSITORY CORE FILE)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pfiles -n -c &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; procfiles_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;truss &amp;ndash;d &amp;ndash;vall &amp;ndash;fall &amp;ndash;o truss_pmrepagent_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;.out &amp;ndash;p &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; (ONLY ON THE REPOSITORY AND NOT THE NODE JAVA)&lt;br /&gt;Let this run for around two minutes and then exit.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Collect the following(these do not require a process ID)&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;netstat &amp;gt; netstat_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt; Taken at least three times&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;vmstat 5 5 &amp;gt; vmstat_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;iostat 5 5 &amp;gt; iostat_otput&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;prstat 5 5 &amp;gt; prstat_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;sar -A &amp;gt; sar_output&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;If SAR does not work, check if the system has nmon installed.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;/&lt;span&gt;var/adm/messages file.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Collect the following logs:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;pmap, gcore, pfiles, truss, netstat, vmstat, prstat, sar, nmon are all Solaris system utilities. In case of any issues, contact your system admins.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;pmstack is available under $INFA_HOME/tools/debugtools/pmstack directory in Informatica installations version 9.5.x and above. For other versions it could be downloaded from &lt;a title=&quot;pmstack&quot; href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/docs/DOC-7327&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here.&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;jstack and jmap are present in $JAVA_HOME/bin/ directory.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#c298b5b0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c291b0d0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backc298b5b0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#c291b0d0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;The first step is to get the Process ID(PID) of the repository service. If there is just one repository service running on the server you can easily get the PID by logging into the machine and checking for the running processes. The repository service runs as a &quot;pmrepagent&quot; process. If there are multiple Repository service processes you can get the Process ID from the admin console's &quot;Logs&quot; tab. Just filter the logs for the repository service in question here and then add the &quot;Node&quot; and &quot;Process&quot; columns to the already available columns in the log window(you can do that by doing a Right click on any of the columns viz. Service Type, Service Name etc and then clicking on Columns). This would give you the node on which the process is running as well as the Process ID with which the service is running. Please refer to KB &lt;a title=&quot;KB151366_Find_PID&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/151366.aspx?myk=151366&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;151366&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for other options.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;We also need to get the Process ID of the node java process. <div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Once you have the PID of the pmrepagent process and the node java process, following should be run:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;pmap &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; pmap_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jstack &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; jstack_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt; (ONLY ON THE NODE JAVA AND NOT THE REPOSITORY)&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;gcore &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file generated in the above step. Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;http://psv28cmsmas1:7000/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more information. &lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jmap -dump:format=b,file=heapdump.core.&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;lt;EXECUTABLE NAME AND PATH&amp;gt; &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt; (ONLY ON THE NODE JAVA CORE FILE AND NOT THE REPOSITORY CORE FILE)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pfiles -n -c &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; procfiles_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;truss &amp;ndash;d &amp;ndash;vall &amp;ndash;fall &amp;ndash;o truss_pmrepagent_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;.out &amp;ndash;p &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; (ONLY ON THE REPOSITORY AND NOT THE NODE JAVA)&lt;br /&gt;Let this run for around two minutes and then exit.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Collect the following(these do not require a process ID)&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;netstat &amp;gt; netstat_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt; Taken at least three times&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;vmstat 5 5 &amp;gt; vmstat_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;iostat 5 5 &amp;gt; iostat_otput&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;prstat 5 5 &amp;gt; prstat_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;sar -A &amp;gt; sar_output&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;If SAR does not work, check if the system has nmon installed.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;/&lt;span&gt;var/adm/messages file.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Collect the following logs:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

For other versions it could be downloaded from &lt;a title=&quot;pmstack&quot; href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/docs/DOC-7327&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here.&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;c28fdc10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Solaris/SunOS&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#c295cf80-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c28fdc10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backc295cf80-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#c28fdc10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div&gt;The first step is to identify the admin console process ID. You can run the below command to find the admin console PID:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;&lt;em&gt;ps -fe | grep &amp;lt;username&amp;gt; | grep _AdminConsole&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Contrary to the popular belief Admin console process CAN run on a non-mastergateway node as well(it however CANNOT run on a worker node), so if the domain had multiple gateway nodes, please check for the admin console process on all the gateway nodes if we are unable to find it on the master gateway.&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Next step is to find the PID of the node java process of the master gateway node(If the admin console is running on a non-masterGateway node also get the Process ID of the node process of that node. This would be the parent process of the admin console process). Refer to the KB &lt;a title=&quot;147825 find node java PID&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/147825.aspx?myk=147825&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;147825&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;to get the PID of the node java process of the master gateway node.&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Once you have the PIDs, run the following diagnostics:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -p -d dbx &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at an interval of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmap &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; pmap_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jstack &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; jstack_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_n.out&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;gcore &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file generated in the above step. Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;http://psv28cmsmas1:7000/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more information. &lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jmap -dump:format=b,file=heapdump.core.&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;lt;EXECUTABLE NAME AND PATH&amp;gt; &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pfiles &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; pfiles_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;truss &amp;ndash;d &amp;ndash;vall &amp;ndash;fall &amp;ndash;o truss_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;.out -p &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Let this run for around two minutes and then exit.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Collect the following(these do not require a process ID)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;netstat &amp;gt; netstat_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt; Taken at least three times&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;vmstat 5 5 &amp;gt; vmstat_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;iostat 5 5 &amp;gt; iostat_otput&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;prstat 5 5 &amp;gt; prstat_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;sar -A &amp;gt; sar_output&amp;nbsp;If SAR does not work, check if the system has nmon installed.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;/var/adm/messages file.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Collect the following logs:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>infa9Logs on all the nodes of the domain. Please click &lt;a title=&quot;infa9Logs&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/147882.aspx?myk=147882&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for details on the utility. </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;pmap, gcore, pfiles, truss, netstat, vmstat, prstat, sar, nmon are all Solaris system utilities. In case of any issues, contact your system admins.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;pmstack is available under&lt;em&gt; $INFA_HOME/tools/debugtools/pmstack&lt;/em&gt; directory in Informatica installations version 9.5.x and above. For other versions it could be downloaded from &lt;a title=&quot;pmstack&quot; href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/docs/DOC-7327&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here.&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;jstack and jmap are present in &lt;em&gt;$JAVA_HOME/bin/ &lt;/em&gt;directory.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#c295f690-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c28fdc10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backc295f690-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#c28fdc10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div&gt;The first step is to identify the admin console process ID. You can run the below command to find the admin console PID:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;&lt;em&gt;ps -fe | grep &amp;lt;username&amp;gt; | grep _AdminConsole&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Contrary to the popular belief Admin console process CAN run on a non-mastergateway node as well(it however CANNOT run on a worker node), so if the domain had multiple gateway nodes, please check for the admin console process on all the gateway nodes if we are unable to find it on the master gateway.&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Next step is to find the PID of the node java process of the master gateway node(If the admin console is running on a non-masterGateway node also get the Process ID of the node process of that node. This would be the parent process of the admin console process). Refer to the KB &lt;a title=&quot;147825 find node java PID&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/147825.aspx?myk=147825&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;147825&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;to get the PID of the node java process of the master gateway node.&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Once you have the PIDs, run the following diagnostics:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -p -d dbx &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at an interval of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmap &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; pmap_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jstack &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; jstack_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_n.out&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;gcore &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file generated in the above step. Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;http://psv28cmsmas1:7000/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more information. &lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jmap -dump:format=b,file=heapdump.core.&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;lt;EXECUTABLE NAME AND PATH&amp;gt; &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pfiles &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; pfiles_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;truss &amp;ndash;d &amp;ndash;vall &amp;ndash;fall &amp;ndash;o truss_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;.out -p &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Let this run for around two minutes and then exit.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Collect the following(these do not require a process ID)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;netstat &amp;gt; netstat_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt; Taken at least three times&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;vmstat 5 5 &amp;gt; vmstat_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;iostat 5 5 &amp;gt; iostat_otput&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;prstat 5 5 &amp;gt; prstat_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;sar -A &amp;gt; sar_output&amp;nbsp;If SAR does not work, check if the system has nmon installed.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;/var/adm/messages file.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Collect the following logs:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>infa9Logs on all the nodes of the domain. Please click &lt;a title=&quot;infa9Logs&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/147882.aspx?myk=147882&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for details on the utility. </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;pmap, gcore, pfiles, truss, netstat, vmstat, prstat, sar, nmon are all Solaris system utilities. In case of any issues, contact your system admins.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;pmstack is available under&lt;em&gt; $INFA_HOME/tools/debugtools/pmstack&lt;/em&gt; directory in Informatica installations version 9.5.x and above. For other versions it could be downloaded from &lt;a title=&quot;pmstack&quot; href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/docs/DOC-7327&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here.&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;jstack and jmap are present in &lt;em&gt;$JAVA_HOME/bin/ &lt;/em&gt;directory.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backc28fdc10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c28fdc10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#c28ea390-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c28fdc10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;51fec3d0-8dfa-11e6-a94c-bc764e10d166&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Linux&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;The first step is to find the Process ID of the node that is hung and the PID of the master gateway node Java process. The node process would be the Parent process of all the other application services running on the node.&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;To find the master gateway node, if you have multiple gateway nodes in the domain, you would need to check the &lt;em&gt;catalina.out&lt;/em&gt; file present in the &lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/tomcat/logs/ directory&lt;/em&gt; (in case of all Informatica 9.x versions) or &lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/logs/&amp;lt;NODE_NAME&amp;gt;/ &lt;/em&gt;directory(in Informatica 10.x versions). The Master gateway node would have a log entry like &quot;Master Core services enabled.&quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;For more details on finding the PID, refer KB &lt;a title=&quot;147825 find node java PID&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/147825.aspx?myk=147825&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;147825.&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Once you have the PIDs, run the following diagnostics:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -p -d dbx &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at an interval of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmap &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; pmap_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jstack &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; jstack_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;gcore &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file generated in the above step. Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;http://psv28cmsmas1:7000/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more information.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jmap -dump:format=b,file=heapdump.core.&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;lt;EXECUTABLE NAME AND PATH&amp;gt; &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;lsof -p &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; lsof_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;strace -fF -tT -all -o strace_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;.out -p &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Let this run for around two minutes and then exit.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Collect the following(these do not require a process ID)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;netstat &amp;gt; netstat_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt; Taken at least three times&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;vmstat 5 5 &amp;gt; vmstat_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;iostat 5 5 &amp;gt; iostat_otput&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;top &amp;ndash;d 5 &amp;ndash;n 5 &amp;gt; top_out&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;sar -A &amp;gt; sar_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;/var/log/messages file.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Collect the following logs:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>infa9Logs on the node which is hung and on the master gateway node. Click &lt;a title=&quot;infa9Logs&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/147882.aspx?myk=147882&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for details on the utility.</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;pmap, gcore, lsof, truss, netstat, vmstat, top, sar, are all Linux system utilities. In case of any issues, contact your system admins.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;pmstack is available under&lt;em&gt; $INFA_HOME/tools/debugtools/pmstack &lt;/em&gt;directory in Informatica installations version 9.5.x and above. For other versions it could be downloaded from &lt;a title=&quot;pmstack&quot; href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/docs/DOC-7327&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here.&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;jstack and jmap are present in $JAVA_HOME/bin/ directory.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Did you face any issues while collecting the above?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#644b5fa0-8de4-11e6-a94c-bc764e10d166&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c28ecaa0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back644b5fa0-8de4-11e6-a94c-bc764e10d166').attr('href', '#c28ecaa0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;While using an UNIX-based system, run the following command that works on all the supported Operating Systems to find the Operating System:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;uname -a&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#67eacd80-8de4-11e6-ae58-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c28ecaa0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back67eacd80-8de4-11e6-ae58-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#c28ecaa0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;While using an UNIX-based system, run the following command that works on all the supported Operating Systems to find the Operating System:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;uname -a&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#6b376070-8de4-11e6-ae58-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c28ecaa0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back6b376070-8de4-11e6-ae58-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#c28ecaa0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;While using an UNIX-based system, run the following command that works on all the supported Operating Systems to find the Operating System:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;uname -a&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#6ee1f1e0-8de4-11e6-9788-bc764e11d2f4&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c28ecaa0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back6ee1f1e0-8de4-11e6-9788-bc764e11d2f4').attr('href', '#c28ecaa0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;While using an UNIX-based system, run the following command that works on all the supported Operating Systems to find the Operating System:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;uname -a&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backc28ecaa0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c28ecaa0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#c28ea390-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c28ecaa0-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;c295a870-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Solaris&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;The first step is to identify the admin console process ID. You can run the below command to find the admin console PID:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;&lt;em&gt;ps -fe | grep &amp;lt;username&amp;gt; | grep _AdminConsole&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Contrary to the popular belief Admin console process CAN run on a non-mastergateway node as well(it however CANNOT run on a worker node), so if the domain had multiple gateway nodes, please check for the admin console process on all the gateway nodes if we are unable to find it on the master gateway.&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Next step is to find the PID of the node java process of the master gateway node(If the admin console is running on a non-masterGateway node also get the Process ID of the node process of that node. This would be the parent process of the admin console process). Refer to the KB &lt;a title=&quot;147825 find node java PID&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/147825.aspx?myk=147825&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;147825&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;to get the PID of the node java process of the master gateway node.&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Once you have the PIDs, run the following diagnostics:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -p -d dbx &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at an interval of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmap &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; pmap_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jstack &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; jstack_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_n.out&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;gcore &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file generated in the above step. Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;http://psv28cmsmas1:7000/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more information. &lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jmap -dump:format=b,file=heapdump.core.&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;lt;EXECUTABLE NAME AND PATH&amp;gt; &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pfiles &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; pfiles_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;truss &amp;ndash;d &amp;ndash;vall &amp;ndash;fall &amp;ndash;o truss_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;.out -p &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Let this run for around two minutes and then exit.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Collect the following(these do not require a process ID)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;netstat &amp;gt; netstat_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt; Taken at least three times&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;vmstat 5 5 &amp;gt; vmstat_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;iostat 5 5 &amp;gt; iostat_otput&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;prstat 5 5 &amp;gt; prstat_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;sar -A &amp;gt; sar_output&amp;nbsp;If SAR does not work, check if the system has nmon installed.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;/var/adm/messages file.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Collect the following logs:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>infa9Logs on all the nodes of the domain. Please click &lt;a title=&quot;infa9Logs&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/147882.aspx?myk=147882&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for details on the utility. </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;pmap, gcore, pfiles, truss, netstat, vmstat, prstat, sar, nmon are all Solaris system utilities. In case of any issues, contact your system admins.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;pmstack is available under&lt;em&gt; $INFA_HOME/tools/debugtools/pmstack&lt;/em&gt; directory in Informatica installations version 9.5.x and above. For other versions it could be downloaded from &lt;a title=&quot;pmstack&quot; href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/docs/DOC-7327&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here.&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;jstack and jmap are present in &lt;em&gt;$JAVA_HOME/bin/ &lt;/em&gt;directory.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;No&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backc2984080-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c2984080-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; href=&quot;#c28ea390-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c2984080-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;426a0390-8de5-11e6-9788-bc764e11d2f4&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;AIX&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;The first step is to find the Process ID of the node that is hung and the PID of the master gateway node java process. The node process would be the Parent process of all the other application services running on the node.&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;To find the master gateway node, if you have multiple gateway nodes in the domain, you would need to check the &lt;em&gt;catalina.out&lt;/em&gt; file present in the &lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/tomcat/logs/ directory&lt;/em&gt; (in case of all Informatica 9.x versions) or &lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/logs/&amp;lt;NODE_NAME&amp;gt;/&lt;/em&gt; directory (in Informatica 10.x versions). The Master gateway node would have a log entry like &quot;Master Core services enabled.&quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;For more details on finding the PID, refer KB &lt;a title=&quot;147825 find node java PID&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/147825.aspx?myk=147825&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;147825.&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Once we have the PIDs we need to run the following diagnostics&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -p -d dbx &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at an interval of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;procmap &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; procmap_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;kill -QUIT &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; (THIS WILL GENERATE FILES WITH THE NAME javacore.* IN $INFA_HOME/tomcat/bin/)&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;gencore &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file generated in the above step. Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;http://psv28cmsmas1:7000/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more information. &lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jextract &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt; jextract_&amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;procfiles -n -c &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; procfiles_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;truss -D -d -i -l -f -o truss_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;.out -p &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Let this run for around two minutes and then exit.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;&lt;ol&gt; &lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Collect the following(these do not require a process ID)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;netstat &amp;gt; netstat_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt; Taken at least three times&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;vmstat 5 5 &amp;gt; vmstat_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;iostat 5 5 &amp;gt; iostat_otput&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;svmon -l 60 60 &amp;gt; svmon_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;sar -A &amp;gt; sar_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;errpt -a &amp;gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;errpr_aix.txt&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Collect the following logs:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;infa9Logs on the node which is hung and on the master gateway node. Click &lt;a title=&quot;infa9Logs&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/147882.aspx?myk=147882&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for details on the utility.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;procmap, gencore, procfiles, truss, netstat, vmstat, svmon, sar, errpt are all AIX system utilities. In case of any issues, contact your system admins.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;pmstack is available under &lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/tools/debugtools/pmstack &lt;/em&gt;directory in Informatica installations version 9.5.x and above. For other versions, it could be downloaded from &lt;a title=&quot;pmstack&quot; href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/docs/DOC-7327&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here.&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;jextract is present in&lt;em&gt; $JAVA_HOME/jre/bin/&lt;/em&gt; directory.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Did you face any issues while collecting the above?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot;
