<div>&lt;li&gt;gencore &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file generated in the above step. Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;http://psv28cmsmas1:7000/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more information. &lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jextract &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt; jextract_core (ONLY ON THE NODE JAVA CORE FILE AND NOT THE REPOSITORY CORE FILE &lt;span&gt;OR INTEGRATION SERVICE CORE&lt;/span&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;procfiles -n -c &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; procfiles_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;truss -D -d -i -l -f -o truss_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;.out -p &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; (ONLY ON THE REPOSITORY, INTEGRATION SERVICE AND NOT THE NODE JAVA)&lt;br /&gt;Let this run for around two minutes and then exit.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt; &lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Collect the following(these do not require a process ID)&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;netstat &amp;gt; netstat_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt; Taken at least three times&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;vmstat 5 5 &amp;gt; vmstat_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;iostat 5 5 &amp;gt; iostat_otput&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;svmon -l 60 60 &amp;gt; svmon_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;sar -A &amp;gt; sar_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;errpt -a &amp;gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;errpr_aix.txt&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Collect the following logs:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Integration service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;procmap, gencore, procfiles, truss, netstat, vmstat, svmon, sar, errpt are all AIX system utilities. In case of any issues, contact your system admins.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;pmstack is available under $INFA_HOME/tools/debugtools/pmstack directory in Informatica installations version 9.5.x and above. For other versions it could be downloaded from &lt;a title=&quot;pmstack&quot; href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/docs/DOC-7327&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here.&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;jextract is present in $JAVA_HOME/jre/bin/ directory.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Did you face any issues while collecting the above?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#c294be10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#bc845a50-8d1c-11e6-8814-bc764e10d166').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backc294be10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#bc845a50-8d1c-11e6-8814-bc764e10d166');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Yes&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#c294e520-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#bc845a50-8d1c-11e6-8814-bc764e10d166').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backc294e520-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#bc845a50-8d1c-11e6-8814-bc764e10d166');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;No&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backbc845a50-8d1c-11e6-8814-bc764e10d166&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#bc845a50-8d1c-11e6-8814-bc764e10d166').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#c28ea390-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#bc845a50-8d1c-11e6-8814-bc764e10d166').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;c2977d30-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backc2977d30-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c2977d30-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#c28ea390-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c2977d30-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;c2905140-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Linux&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;The first step is to identify the admin console process ID. You can run the below command to find the admin console PID:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;&lt;em&gt;ps -fe | grep &amp;lt;username&amp;gt; | grep _AdminConsole&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Contrary to the popular belief Admin console process CAN run on a non-mastergateway node as well(it however CANNOT run on a worker node), so if the domain had multiple gateway nodes, please check for the admin console process on all the gateway nodes if we are unable to find it on the master gateway.&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Next step is to find the PID of the node java process of the master gateway node(If the admin console is running on a non-masterGateway node also get the Process ID of the node process of that node. This would be the parent process of the admin console process). Refer to the KB &lt;a title=&quot;147825 find node java PID&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/147825.aspx?myk=147825&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;147825&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;to get the PID of the node java process of the master gateway node.&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Once you have the PIDs, run the following diagnostics:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -p -d dbx &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at an interval of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmap &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; pmap_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jstack &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; jstack_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;gcore &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file generated in the above step. Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;http://psv28cmsmas1:7000/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more information. &lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jmap -dump:format=b,file=heapdump.core.&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;lt;EXECUTABLE NAME AND PATH&amp;gt; &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;lsof -p &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; lsof_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;strace -fF -tT -all -o strace_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;.out -p &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Let this run for around two minutes and then exit.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Collect the following(these do not require a process ID)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;netstat &amp;gt; netstat_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt; Taken at least three times&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;vmstat 5 5 &amp;gt; vmstat_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;iostat 5 5 &amp;gt; iostat_otput&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;top &amp;ndash;d 5 &amp;ndash;n 5 &amp;gt; top_out&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;sar -A &amp;gt; sar_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;/var/log/messages file.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Collect the following logs:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;infa9Logs on all the nodes of the domain. Please click &lt;a title=&quot;infa9Logs&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/147882.aspx?myk=147882&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for details on the utility.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;pmap, gcore, lsof, truss, netstat, vmstat, top, sar, are all Linux system utilities. In case of any issues, contact your system admins.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;pmstack is available under&lt;em&gt; $INFA_HOME/tools/debugtools/pmstack&lt;/em&gt; directory in Informatica installations version 9.5.x and above. For other versions it could be downloaded from &lt;a title=&quot;pmstack&quot; href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/docs/DOC-7327&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here.&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;jstack and jmap are present in &lt;em&gt;$JAVA_HOME/bin/ &lt;/em&gt;directory.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Did you face any issues while collecting the above?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#c294be10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c2905140-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backc294be10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#c2905140-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Yes&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#c294e520-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c2905140-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backc294e520-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#c2905140-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;No&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backc2905140-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c2905140-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#c28ea390-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c2905140-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;c2924d10-6056-11e5-a8b7-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Linux&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;The first step is to get the Process ID(PID) of the repository service. If there is just one repository service running on the server you can easily get the PID by logging into the machine and checking for the running processes. The repository service runs as a &quot;pmrepagent&quot; process. If there are multiple Repository service processes you can get the Process ID from the admin console's &quot;Logs&quot; tab. Just filter the logs for the repository service in question here and then add the &quot;Node&quot; and &quot;Process&quot; columns to the already available columns in the log window(you can do that by doing a Right click on any of the columns viz. Service Type, Service Name etc and then clicking on Columns). This would give you the node on which the process is running as well as the Process ID with which the service is running. Please refer to KB &lt;a title=&quot;KB151366_Find_PID&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/151366.aspx?myk=151366&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;151366&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for other options.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;We also need to get the Process ID of the node java process. You can login to the node running the master gateway process and get the PID of a java process which is the Parent of the repository service process that we just found and that would be the PID of the node java. If you have a multinode setup and the repository service is running on a node other than the master gateway, you would require two Process IDs, one for the parent of the pmrepagent we just found and the other for the node java process of the master gateway node. For more details on how to get the PID, please refer to KB &lt;a title=&quot;147825 find node java PID&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/6/Pages/1/147825.aspx?myk=147825&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;147825&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;One you have the PID of the pmrepagent process and the node java process, following should be run:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Execute the following on the PID of the pmrepagent process and the node java process.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -p -d dbx &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at an interval of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmap &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; pmap_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jstack &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; jstack_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt; (ONLY ON THE NODE JAVA AND NOT THE REPOSITORY)&lt;br /&gt;Taken three times at a gap of 30 seconds.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;gcore &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;  </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file generated in the above step. Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;http://psv28cmsmas1:7000/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more information. &lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jmap -dump:format=b,file=heapdump.core.&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;lt;EXECUTABLE NAME AND PATH&amp;gt; &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt; (ONLY ON THE NODE JAVA CORE FILE AND NOT THE REPOSITORY CORE FILE)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;lsof -p &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; &amp;gt; lsof_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;strace -fF -tT -all -o strace_&amp;lt;PID&amp;gt;.out -p &amp;lt;PID&amp;gt; (ONLY ON THE REPOSITORY AND NOT THE NODE JAVA)  </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Let this run for around two minutes and then exit.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt; &lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Collect the following(these do not require a process ID)&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;netstat &amp;gt; netstat_&amp;lt;n&amp;gt; Taken at least three times&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;vmstat 5 5 &amp;gt; vmstat_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;iostat 5 5 &amp;gt; iostat_otput&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;top &amp;ndash;d 5 &amp;ndash;n 5 &amp;gt; top_out&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;sar -A &amp;gt; sar_output&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;/var/log/messages file.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Collect the following logs:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;pmap, gcore, lsof, truss, netstat, vmstat, top, sar, are all Linux system utilities. In case of any issues, contact your system admins.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;pmstack is available under $INFA_HOME/tools/debugtools/pmstack directory in Informatica installations version 9.5.x and above. For other versions it could be downloaded from &lt;a title=&quot;pmstack&quot; href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/docs/DOC-7327&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here.&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
